### 3. We are only interested in code, sex, weight, year of birth. Restrict the data to these variables and store the datafame as a new object. 

```r
bison_new <- select(bison, "animal_code", "animal_sex", "animal_weight", "animal_yob")
```


```r
bison %>%
  select(animal_code, animal_sex, animal_weight, animal_yob)
```

### 4. Pull out the animals born between 1980-1990. 


```r
filter(bison_new, between(animal_yob, 1980, 1990))
```

### 6. Between 1980-1990, were males or females larger on average? 


```r
males <- filter(bison_new, animal_sex=="M")
```


```r
mean(males$animal_weight, na.rm = T)
```

```
## [1] 727.8503
```


```r
females <- filter(bison_new, animal_sex=="F")
```


```r
mean(females$animal_weight)
```

```
## [1] 761.8764
```
